PLAN:
  === ENVIRONMENT SETUP PLAN (ADJUSTED FOR x86_64 CPU, NO GPU, CPU-ONLY UBUNTU ENV, DEEP PROJECT DIR) ===
  **Summary of Key Adjustments:**
  - All references to CUDA, GPU acceleration, or NVIDIA GPU-specific steps are removed/disabled.
  - All Docker instructions use amd64/x86_64-compatible base images. No nvidia/cuda base images are used.
  - All instructions assume CPU-only operation; any optional GPU flags (e.g., --gpus) are omitted.
  - OS-level instructions and dependencies are targeted to Ubuntu 20.04+ (x86_64) and compatible with macOS/WSL2/Windows (CPU-only).
  - Emphasize large disk requirement for LiveCodeBench-X and large benchmarks.
  - All file paths and scripts must respect deep working directory structure (`/home/cc/EnvGym/data/20260501_153628_tensorblock_gpt-4.1/NeMo_Gym`).
  - All instructions and test cases are reviewed for feasibility on CPU-only x86_64.
  - If any tool or benchmark has an explicit GPU requirement, note that only CPU operation is possible and results may be slower.
  ---
  1. DOWNLOADS NEEDED:
     - **Git**: For cloning repositories.  
       - Version: Latest stable, x86_64/amd64  
       - Install: `sudo apt install git` (Ubuntu) or use system package manager.
     - **Python**: Version 3.12 (required by `.python-version`)  
       - Must be x86_64 build, compatible with Ubuntu 20.04+/macOS/WSL2/Windows.  
       - For Docker, base image should be `python:3.12-slim` or `ubuntu:20.04` with Python 3.12 installed (NOT CUDA or nvidia/cuda images).
     - **UV (Python package manager)**: Latest version (`>=0.9.30`)  
       - Install as before, works on x86_64/amd64.
     - **All Python/Pip Dependencies**:  
       - All libraries listed in the plan are compatible with Python 3.12 and CPU-only operation.  
       - For `mlflow`, `uvicorn`, `uvloop`, `datasets`, `ray`, etc: Only CPU features will be used.  
       - For `ray`, use CPU scheduler (no `--num-gpus`/`--use-gpu` flags).
     - **Docker**:  
       - Use x86_64/amd64 base images (e.g., `python:3.12-slim`, `ubuntu:20.04`).  
       - Do not use any `nvidia/cuda` or `pytorch/pytorch` GPU image.  
       - No `--gpus` flags in `docker run` or `docker build`.  
       - All Dockerfiles should begin with `FROM python:3.12-slim` or similar.  
       - Add `--platform=linux/amd64` to `docker build` if running on multi-arch builder.
     - **NeMo Skills Sandbox**:  
       - Docker build is supported, but image must be built for CPU (`python:3.12`, `ubuntu:20.04`, etc).  
       - If upstream Dockerfile refers to CUDA or NVIDIA drivers, you must edit it to use CPU-only base and remove GPU-specific instructions.  
       - Example:  
         ```dockerfile
         FROM python:3.12-slim
         # ... rest of Dockerfile ...
         # (No CUDA install, no NVIDIA driver steps)
         ```
     - **All Benchmarks**:  
       - All benchmarks can run in CPU-only mode, but may be slower (especially for large models like vLLM).
       - vLLM, large model serving, and code generation will run in CPU mode only.
       - For any model serving, ensure that server is launched with CPU-only backend or CPU-compatible weights.
       - For asr_with_pc, code_gen, judge servers, etc: Ensure they are run in CPU mode.
     - **Storage Space**:  
       - LiveCodeBench-X and other large benchmarks may require 20+ GB free disk space in the working directory/subfolders.
       - Ensure `/home/cc/EnvGym/data/20260501_153628_tensorblock_gpt-4.1/NeMo_Gym` has sufficient disk space for large data files and outputs.
     - **Other OS Tools**:  
       - All instructions use CPU-only tools, compatible with Ubuntu 20.04+.
       - No GPU drivers or CUDA dependencies are required/installed.
  2. FILES TO CREATE:
     - All file locations are relative to `/home/cc/EnvGym/data/20260501_153628_tensorblock_gpt-4.1/NeMo_Gym`.
     - No files or scripts should assume `/home/cc` is writable by root or Docker (unless explicitly bind-mounting).
     - All large data files (e.g., LiveCodeBench-X JSONLs) are stored under this structure; verify sufficient disk space.
     - All other file instructions unchanged.
  3. NECESSARY TEST CASES IN THE CODEBASE:
     - **All tests related to GPU acceleration should be disabled or skipped.**
     - All tests must pass on CPU-only environment.  
     - Test suite should include explicit check that GPU is not required (e.g., `torch.cuda.is_available()` is False, `--gpus` not required).
     - Any tests that check CUDA, NCCL, or GPU-specific logic should be skipped or marked as expected to fail on CPU-only.
     - **Model server startup:**  
       - All tests must start model servers in CPU mode.  
       - vLLM or other model APIs must be started with CPU backend or CPU-compatible weights/config.
       - If a test/benchmark would fail due to lack of GPU, it must emit a clear message indicating "This task requires a GPU to run efficiently. On CPU, it will be slow or may not be feasible for large models." but must not hard-fail.
     - All other test cases as previously specified.

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM python:3.12-slim
  # Set environment vars for non-interactive install, UTF-8, and prompt for Python
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive \
      LC_ALL=C.UTF-8 \
      LANG=C.UTF-8 \
      PYTHONUNBUFFERED=1 \
      PIP_DISABLE_PIP_VERSION_CHECK=on \
      PIP_NO_CACHE_DIR=on
  # Set the deep project workdir
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data/20260501_153628_tensorblock_gpt-4.1/NeMo_Gym
  # Install system dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          git \
          curl \
          build-essential \
          ca-certificates \
          libssl-dev \
          libffi-dev \
          openssh-client \
          gcc \
          make \
          pkg-config \
          libsndfile1 \
          ffmpeg \
          unzip \
          vim \
          less \
          tzdata \
          && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install uv (Python package manager)
  RUN pip install --upgrade pip && \
      pip install 'uv>=0.9.30'
  # Copy python version file if present (for pyenv tooling, if needed)
  COPY .python-version ./
  # (Optional) Pre-copy requirements for layer caching, if requirements file exists
  COPY requirements.txt requirements.txt
  COPY pyproject.toml pyproject.toml
  COPY poetry.lock poetry.lock
  # Create virtual environment in standard location
  # (uv uses its own env management, but we'll also make a venv for CLI compatibility)
  RUN python -m venv /opt/venv && \
      . /opt/venv/bin/activate && \
      pip install --upgrade pip
  ENV VIRTUAL_ENV=/opt/venv
  ENV PATH="/opt/venv/bin:$PATH"
  # Install project dependencies using uv (preferred over pip for speed/caching)
  RUN if [ -f "pyproject.toml" ]; then uv pip install -r requirements.txt || uv pip install . ; \
      elif [ -f "requirements.txt" ]; then uv pip install -r requirements.txt ; \
      fi
  # Install pre-commit
  RUN pip install pre-commit
  # Copy the rest of the repository
  COPY . .
  # Install the repository in editable mode (if applicable)
  RUN if [ -f "pyproject.toml" ]; then uv pip install -e . ; \
      elif [ -f "setup.py" ]; then pip install -e . ; \
      fi
  # Set permissions for the working directory (for non-root bind mounts)
  RUN chmod -R a+rwX /home/cc/EnvGym/data/20260501_153628_tensorblock_gpt-4.1/NeMo_Gym
  # Set the entrypoint to /bin/bash at repository root
  ENTRYPOINT ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM python:3.12-slim
  # Set environment vars for non-interactive install, UTF-8, and prompt for Python
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive \
      LC_ALL=C.UTF-8 \
      LANG=C.UTF-8 \
      PYTHONUNBUFFERED=1 \
      PIP_DISABLE_PIP_VERSION_CHECK=on \
      PIP_NO_CACHE_DIR=on
  # Set the project workdir to repository root
  WORKDIR /workspace
  # Install system dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          git \
          curl \
          build-essential \
          ca-certificates \
          libssl-dev \
          libffi-dev \
          openssh-client \
          gcc \
          make \
          pkg-config \
          libsndfile1 \
          ffmpeg \
          unzip \
          vim \
          less \
          tzdata \
          && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install uv (Python package manager)
  RUN pip install --upgrade pip && \
      pip install 'uv>=0.9.30'
  # Copy python version file if present (for pyenv tooling, if needed)
  COPY .python-version ./
  # (Optional) Pre-copy requirements for layer caching, if requirements file exists
  COPY requirements.txt requirements.txt
  COPY pyproject.toml pyproject.toml
  # Create virtual environment in standard location
  # (uv uses its own env management, but we'll also make a venv for CLI compatibility)
  RUN python -m venv /opt/venv && \
      . /opt/venv/bin/activate && \
      pip install --upgrade pip
  ENV VIRTUAL_ENV=/opt/venv
  ENV PATH="/opt/venv/bin:$PATH"
  # Install project dependencies using uv (preferred over pip for speed/caching)
  RUN if [ -f "pyproject.toml" ]; then uv pip install -r requirements.txt || uv pip install . ; \
      elif [ -f "requirements.txt" ]; then uv pip install -r requirements.txt ; \
      fi
  # Install pre-commit
  RUN pip install pre-commit
  # Copy the rest of the repository
  COPY . .
  # Install the repository in editable mode (if applicable)
  RUN if [ -f "pyproject.toml" ]; then uv pip install -e . ; \
      elif [ -f "setup.py" ]; then pip install -e . ; \
      fi
  # Set permissions for the working directory (for non-root bind mounts)
  RUN chmod -R a+rwX /workspace
  # Set the entrypoint to /bin/bash at repository root
  ENTRYPOINT ["/bin/bash"]

  FROM python:3.12-slim
  # Set environment vars for non-interactive install, UTF-8, and prompt for Python
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive \
      LC_ALL=C.UTF-8 \
      LANG=C.UTF-8 \
      PYTHONUNBUFFERED=1 \
      PIP_DISABLE_PIP_VERSION_CHECK=on \
      PIP_NO_CACHE_DIR=on
  # Set the project workdir to repository root
  WORKDIR /workspace
  # Install system dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          git \
          curl \
          build-essential \
          ca-certificates \
          libssl-dev \
          libffi-dev \
          openssh-client \
          gcc \
          make \
          pkg-config \
          libsndfile1 \
          ffmpeg \
          unzip \
          vim \
          less \
          tzdata \
          && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install uv (Python package manager)
  RUN pip install --upgrade pip && \
      pip install 'uv>=0.9.30'
  # Copy python version file if present (for pyenv tooling, if needed)
  COPY .python-version ./
  # Copy pyproject.toml (requirements.txt does NOT exist, so do not copy it)
  COPY pyproject.toml pyproject.toml
  # Create virtual environment in standard location
  RUN python -m venv /opt/venv && \
      . /opt/venv/bin/activate && \
      pip install --upgrade pip
  ENV VIRTUAL_ENV=/opt/venv
  ENV PATH="/opt/venv/bin:$PATH"
  # Install project dependencies using uv (only pyproject.toml exists)
  RUN if [ -f "pyproject.toml" ]; then uv pip install . ; fi
  # Install pre-commit
  RUN pip install pre-commit
  # Copy the rest of the repository
  COPY . .
  # Install the repository in editable mode (if applicable)
  RUN if [ -f "pyproject.toml" ]; then uv pip install -e . ; \
      elif [ -f "setup.py" ]; then pip install -e . ; \
      fi
  # Set permissions for the working directory (for non-root bind mounts)
  RUN chmod -R a+rwX /workspace
  # Set the entrypoint to /bin/bash at repository root
  ENTRYPOINT ["/bin/bash"]

  **Summary of Key Adjustments:**
  - All references to CUDA, GPU acceleration, or NVIDIA GPU-specific steps are removed/disabled.
  - All Docker instructions use amd64/x86_64-compatible base images. No nvidia/cuda base images are used.
  - All instructions assume CPU-only operation; any optional GPU flags (e.g., --gpus) are omitted.
  - OS-level instructions and dependencies are targeted to Ubuntu 20.04+ (x86_64) and compatible with macOS/WSL2/Windows (CPU-only).
  - Emphasize large disk requirement for LiveCodeBench-X and large benchmarks.
  - All file paths and scripts must respect deep working directory structure (`/home/cc/EnvGym/data/20260501_153628_tensorblock_gpt-4.1/NeMo_Gym`).
  - All instructions and test cases are reviewed for feasibility on CPU-only x86_64.
  - If any tool or benchmark has an explicit GPU requirement, note that only CPU operation is possible and results may be slower.
  ---
  1. DOWNLOADS NEEDED:
     - **Git**: For cloning repositories.  
       - Version: Latest stable, x86_64/amd64

       - For `mlflow`, `uvicorn`, `uvloop`, `datasets`, `ray`, etc: Only CPU features will be used.

       - Use x86_64/amd64 base images (e.g., `python:3.12-slim`, `ubuntu:20.04`).  
       - Do not use any `nvidia/cuda` or `pytorch/pytorch` GPU image.  
       - No `--gpus` flags in `docker run` or `docker build`.  
       - All Dockerfiles should begin with `FROM python:3.12-slim` or similar.  
       - Add `--platform=linux/amd64` to `docker build` if running on multi-arch builder.
     - **NeMo Skills Sandbox**:  
       - Docker build is supported, but image must be built for CPU (`python:3.12`, `ubuntu:20.04`, etc).  
       - If upstream Dockerfile refers to CUDA or NVIDIA drivers, you must edit it to use CPU-only base and remove GPU-specific instructions.  
       - Example:  
         ```dockerfile
         FROM python:3.12-slim
         # ... rest of Dockerfile ...
         # (No CUDA install, no NVIDIA driver steps)
         ```
     - **All Benchmarks**:  
       - All benchmarks can run in CPU-only mode, but may be slower (especially for large models like vLLM).
       - vLLM, large model serving, and code generation will run in CPU mode only.
       - For any model serving, ensure that server is launched with CPU-only backend or CPU-compatible weights.
       - For asr_with_pc, code_gen, judge servers, etc: Ensure they are run in CPU mode.
     - **Storage Space**:  
       - LiveCodeBench-X and other large benchmarks may require 20+ GB free disk space in the working directory/subfolders.
       - Ensure `/home/cc/EnvGym/data/20260501_153628_tensorblock_gpt-4.1/NeMo_Gym` has sufficient disk space for large data files and outputs.
     - **Other OS Tools**:  
       - All instructions use CPU-only tools, compatible with Ubuntu 20.04+.
       - No GPU drivers or CUDA dependencies are required/installed.

     - All file locations are relative to `/home/cc/EnvGym/data/20260501_153628_tensorblock_gpt-4.1/NeMo_Gym`.
     - No files or scripts should assume `/home/cc` is writable by root or Docker (unless explicitly bind-mounting).

  3. NECESSARY TEST CASES IN THE CODEBASE:
     - **All tests related to GPU acceleration should be disabled or skipped.**
     - All tests must pass on CPU-only environment.  
     - Test suite should include explicit check that GPU is not required (e.g., `torch.cuda.is_available()` is False, `--gpus` not required).

  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive \
      LC_ALL=C.UTF-8 \
      LANG=C.UTF-8 \
      PYTHONUNBUFFERED=1 \
      PIP_DISABLE_PIP_VERSION_CHECK=on \
      PIP_NO_CACHE_DIR=on
  WORKDIR /workspace
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          git \
          curl \
          build-essential \
          ca-certificates \
          libssl-dev \
          libffi-dev \
          openssh-client \
          gcc \
          make \
          pkg-config \
          libsndfile1 \
          ffmpeg \
          unzip \
          vim \
          less \
          tzdata \
          && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN pip install --upgrade pip && \
      pip install 'uv>=0.9.30'
  COPY .python-version ./
  COPY pyproject.toml pyproject.toml
  RUN python -m venv /opt/venv && \
      . /opt/venv/bin/activate && \
      pip install --upgrade pip
  ENV VIRTUAL_ENV=/opt/venv
  ENV PATH="/opt/venv/bin:$PATH"
  # Diagnostic: display pyproject.toml content before install
  RUN cat pyproject.toml
  # Copy the rest of the repository before dependency install (so local code is available)
  COPY . .
  # Install build backend explicitly if necessary (setuptools, wheel)
  RUN pip install --upgrade setuptools wheel
  # Install project dependencies with verbose output for diagnostics
  RUN uv pip install --verbose .
  RUN pip install pre-commit
  # Install the repository in editable mode (if applicable)
  RUN if [ -f "pyproject.toml" ]; then uv pip install -e . ; \
      elif [ -f "setup.py" ]; then pip install -e . ; \
      fi
  RUN chmod -R a+rwX /workspace
  ENTRYPOINT ["/bin/bash"]
